   305cc:	e59f0128 	ldr	r0, [pc, #296]	; 306fc <wait_for_tx_complete+0x2c>
    mov r1, #4            // pin_num = 4
   305d0:	e3a01004 	mov	r1, #4
    and r1, r1, #0x1f     // pin_num &= ((1 << 5) - 1)
   305d4:	e201101f 	and	r1, r1, #31
    mov r2, #7            // cfg = 7
   305d8:	e3a02007 	mov	r2, #7
    lsr r3, r1, #3        // (pin_num >> 3)
   305dc:	e1a031a1 	lsr	r3, r1, #3

   305e0:	e1a03103 	lsl	r3, r3, #2

   305e4:	e0803003 	add	r3, r0, r3

   305e8:	e5934000 	ldr	r4, [r3]

   305ec:	e2015007 	and	r5, r1, #7

   305f0:	e1a05105 	lsl	r5, r5, #2
